		   "Hotoda’s Voice", "\"...Headquarter to all cars on standby.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "…目標はバスに乗車せず。",
		   NULL, " ...The target did not board the bus.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "繰り返す。",
		   NULL, " Repeat.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "目標はバスに乗車せず。」",
		   NULL, " The target did not board the bus.\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	OutputLine("織田の声", "「偵察班より本部へ！",
		   "Oda’s Voice", "\"Recon team to headquarters!", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "…停留所、もぬけのからです。",
		   NULL, " ...The bus stop is completely empty.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "失探しました。」",
		   NULL, " We've lost visual!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	OutputLine("新田の声", "「……街道を全て封鎖しろ。",
		   "Nitta’s Voice", "\"......Seal off all the main roads.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "…繰り返す、街道を全て封鎖。",
		   NULL, " ...Repeat, seal off all the main roads.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "…市内へ逃がすなッ！",
		   NULL, " ...Don't let them escape to the city!", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "…生かしたまま捕らえろッ！」",
		   NULL, " ...Capture them alive!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();
	DisableWindow();

	ChangeVolumeOfBGM( 0, 100, 1000 );
	Wait( 1000 );
	StopBGM( 1 );

	Wait( 500 );
	DrawScene( "black", 400 );
	CallScriptSection( "util", "RainOff" );
	DrawScene( "black", 200 );

	GetAchievement("BUSSTOP_4");

	CallScriptSection("&endroll", "BusStopEndRoll");
	//;無線が途切れ、ザーッという砂嵐の音でフェードアウト。\




	//Unhandled subroutine: tei_end_flg


	//Unhandled: reset
}
